components:\\n\\n## Core Interface and Implementation\\n\\nThe **HotRestart interface** is defined in `envoy/server/hot_restart.h` and provides the public API for hot restart operations. The main implementation is **HotRestartImpl** in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` and `source/server/hot_restart_impl.cc`, which coordinates parent and child process communication using shared memory and Unix domain sockets.\\n\\n## Parent/Child Process Handshake\\n\\n**HotRestartingParent** (`source/server/hot_restarting_parent.h/.cc`) handles the parent process side of the hot restart protocol:\\n- Binds to Unix domain sockets and listens for requests from child processes\\n- Exports listener sockets to the child via file descriptor passing (using `sendmsg`/`recvmsg`)\\n- Drains listeners when the child is ready to take over\\n- Exports parent statistics to the child for merging\\n\\n**HotRestartingChild** (`source/server/hot_restarting_child.h/.cc`) handles the child process side:\\n- Connects to parent's Unix domain sockets to request resources\\n- Requests listener socket duplication from the parent\\n- Signals parent when ready to receive connections\\n- Handles parent drained callbacks for UDP listener forwarding\\n\\n## Socket Communication Infrastructure\\n\\n**HotRestartingBase** (`source/server/hot_restarting_base.h/.cc`) provides shared base functionality including the **RpcStream** class, which implements:\\n- Unix domain socket creation and binding using `AF_UNIX, SOCK_DGRAM`\\n- Message sending via `sendmsg()` to pass file descriptors across process boundaries\\n- Message receiving via `recvmsg()` to handle control data with file descriptors\\n- Both main RPC stream and UDP forwarding stream support\\n\\nThe socket communication uses Protocol Buffers defined in `source/server/hot_restart.proto` with **HotRestartMessage** types for child->parent requests and parent->child replies.\\n\\n## Drain Sequence Implementation\\n\\n**DrainManagerImpl** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/.cc`) implements the drain sequence:\\n- Tracks draining state per connection direction (inbound/all)\\n- Creates child drain managers that cascade drain status from parent to child\\n- Manages drain completion callbacks and timeouts\\n- Supports gradual vs. immediate drain strategies\\n- Integrates with listeners to gracefully close connections during hot restart\\n\\n## Shared Memory and Initialization\\n\\n**SharedMemory** structure in `source/server/hot_restart_impl.h` contains:\\n- Synchronization primitives for parent/child coordination\\n- Initialization flags (SHMEM_FLAGS_INITIALIZING)\\n- Memory tracking for hot restart version compatibility\\n- Atomic flags managed via `mmap()` of a named shared memory region\\n\\n## Statistics Merging\\n\\n**StatMerger** (`source/common/stats/stat_merger.h/.cc`) handles merging parent statistics into the child:\\n- Exports gauges and counters from parent process\\n- Child imports and accumulates parent statistics\\n- Handles special stat names like hot_restart_generation\\n\\n## OS System Calls Layer\\n\\n**HotRestartOsSysCalls** (`envoy/api/os_sys_calls_hot_restart.h`) and its POSIX implementation **HotRestartOsSysCallsImpl** (`source/common/api/posix/os_sys_calls_impl_hot_restart.h/.cc`) provide abstracted access to:\\n- Shared memory operations (`shm_open`)\\n- Low-level system calls for the hot restart mechanism\\n\\n## UDP Listener Forwarding\\n\\nSpecialized UDP forwarding support in `source/server/hot_restarting_base.h` includes:\\n- Separate UDP forwarding RPC stream for QUIC packet forwarding\\n- UdpForwardingContext for managing QUIC connections during drain\\n- Listener worker routing for proper packet delivery\\n\\n## Child Process Readiness Signaling\\n\\nChild readiness is signaled through:\\n- **drainParentListeners()** call indicating child is initialized and ready for traffic\\n- **registerParentDrainedCallback()** for listeners to register callbacks when parent drains\\n- **allDrainsImplicitlyComplete()** signaling drain completion\\n- (--base-id, --restart-epoch, --hot-restart-version, etc.)\\n- **Server integration** in `source/exe/stripped_main_base.cc` and `source/exe/main_common.cc` for creating and initializing HotRestartImpl\\n- **Listener management** integration for socket duplication and drain coordination\\n- **Stats export** integration with server statistics stores\\n\\n## Testing\\n\\nComprehensive
